## Information We Collect

We may collect limited technical and usage information such as page views, interaction events, browser/device metadata, and referral information to improve the product experience.

## Analytics Tools

We use analytics providers (such as GA4 and PostHog) to understand traffic and product usage patterns. If your browser blocks analytics scripts, some tracking may not run.

## How We Use Data

We use collected data for product improvements, troubleshooting, feature planning, and performance monitoring. We do not collect unnecessary sensitive personal data through normal site usage.

## Contact

For privacy-related requests, contact [watermeloncorpui@gmail.com](mailto:watermeloncorpui@gmail.com).

## Start a New Project

Initialize a new project using the shadcn CLI:

Next.jsVite

pnpmnpmyarnbun

`npx shadcn@latest init --preset [CODE] --template next`

After project initialization, you can add Watermelon components:

CLIManual

pnpmnpmyarnbun

`npx shadcn@latest add https://registry.watermelon.sh/r/card-split-accordian.json`

## Add to Existing Project

To use Watermelon UI in an existing project, ensure you have **Tailwind CSS v4** and **shadcn-ui** already initialized.

CLIManual

pnpmnpmyarnbun

`npx shadcn@latest add https://registry.watermelon.sh/r/card-split-accordian.json`

## Usage Example

Once installed, you can import and use the component like any other shadcn component.

Usage Example

```
1import { CardSplitAccordian } from "@/components/ui/card-split-accordian";
2
3export default function App() {
4  return (
5    <div className="p-8">
6      <CardSplitAccordian />
7    </div>
8  );
9}
```

## Use of Content

You may browse, copy, and use components from this website in line with the relevant licenses and repository terms. You are responsible for ensuring your own project complies with your legal and licensing needs.

## Inspiration and Originality

We do not intentionally copy proprietary source code from other creators. We may take visual inspiration from publicly shared designs and build implementations ourselves. Where known, we provide credit in the “Inspired By” section.

## Claims and Disputes

If you believe a design or implementation on this site is yours and is being used improperly, email us at [watermeloncorpui@gmail.com](mailto:watermeloncorpui@gmail.com) with proof (original source links, timestamps, repository links, or equivalent evidence).

We will review and resolve valid claims within **7-15 days**. Resolution may include attribution updates, modification, or r%semoval.

## Disclaimer

The website and materials are provided “as is” without warranties of any kind. We are not liable for losses resulting from your use of the site or code.

Apr 14, 2026

1.2.7

Latest

[180New Shadcn Variants](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components)

### Shadcn Variants (Non-Animated)

- Added 180 more non-animated shadcn component variants to significantly expand the component library.

- Focused on performance-friendly, static UI patterns for better usability and faster rendering.

- Maintained consistent styling and structure across all new variants for seamless integration.


### Consistency & Scalability

- Improved scalability of the design system with a larger set of reusable component variations.

- Ensured alignment with existing bento layouts and component ecosystem.

- Enhanced developer experience with more ready-to-use UI building blocks.


Apr 03, 2026

1.2.6

[17New Bento Layouts](https://ui.watermelon.sh/blocks) [170Non-Animated Variants](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components/accordion)

### Bento Layouts

- Introduced modern bento-style layout components for visually rich and structured UI sections.

- Added multiple responsive bento grid variations optimized for dashboards and landing pages.

- Added ready-to-use bento layouts designed for clean structure and modern UI presentation.


### Shadcn Variants (Non-Animated)

- Added non-animated variants for shadcn components to improve performance and accessibility.

- Provided simplified static variants of components for cleaner and distraction-free interfaces.

- Ensured consistent design language across animated and non-animated component sets.


Mar 25, 2026

1.2.5

### Custom Theme Support

- Added support for custom theme CSS variables, allowing users to define their own design system colors.

- Introduced a dedicated theme input panel to apply and preview custom styles in real-time.

- Enabled seamless integration of user-defined themes with base components for consistent UI rendering.

- Improved flexibility for developers to match components with their brand identity using custom variables.


Mar 7, 2026

1.2.4

[128Total Components](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components) [17Total Dashboards](https://ui.watermelon.sh/dashboards)

### New Version: Improvements and New Dashboards

- Fixed bugs and errors across existing components to improve stability and usability.

- Added 5 new components to the registry with polished previews and copy-ready install commands.

- Added 2 new dashboards to the registry with improved functionality and better integration.

- Enhanced functionality across all dashboards for a smoother and more consistent experience.


Feb 22, 2026

1.2.3

[123Total Components](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components) [15New Dashboards](https://ui.watermelon.sh/dashboards) [5New Blocks](https://ui.watermelon.sh/blocks)

### New Version: Added Dashboards and Blocks

- Added 15 new dashboards to the registry with polished previews and copy-ready install commands.

- Added 5 new blocks to the registry with polished previews and copy-ready install commands.

- Added 38 new components to the registry with polished previews and copy-ready install commands.


Feb 15, 2026

1.2.2

[85Total Components](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components)

### Launch

- Watermelon UI is now live with a comprehensive collection of React components.

- launched with 85+ components in the initial release.


Feb 12, 2026

1.2.1

[24Components Added](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components) [6New Categories](https://ui.watermelon.sh/components)

### Components

- Added 24 new components to the registry with polished previews and copy-ready install commands.

- Published full documentation and usage examples for all new additions.


Feb 11, 2026

1.2.0

### Changelog

- Redesigned Changelog page with a modern vertical timeline visualization.

- Integrated Changelog with DocPage components for design consistency.


Feb 10, 2026

1.1.5

### UX & SEO

- Improved SEO with standardized head components and canonical links.

- Added mobile preview restrictions for dashboards and blocks to ensure optimal viewing experience.

- Configured SPA routing for Cloudflare compatibility to fix direct link 404 errors.


### Fixes

- Fixed SVG namespace errors in logo components.

- Converted onboarding components to use NativeWind for better consistency.


Feb 08, 2026

1.1.0

### Performance

- Optimized build performance by switching to PrismLight for syntax highlighting.

`performance``build`

- Refined Vite manualChunks configuration to reduce main bundle size.


### Components

- Added responsive viewer to desktop modals for device preview simulation.


Feb 05, 2026

### Initial Launch

- Watermelon UI is now live with a comprehensive collection of React components, dashboards, and blocks.
